$risque_bg    = $niveau_risque === 'stable' ? 'rgba(111,207,138,.08)' : ($niveau_risque === 'attention' ? 'rgba(240,168,50,.08)' : 'rgba(224,112,112,.08)');
$risque_border= $niveau_risque === 'stable' ? 'rgba(111,207,138,.25)' : ($niveau_risque === 'attention' ? 'rgba(240,168,50,.25)' : 'rgba(224,112,112,.35)');
$risque_label = ['stable'=>'Stable','attention'=>'Attention','critique'=>'Critique'][$niveau_risque] ?? 'Stable';

?>

  <div class="sec-title">Score risque & Prdiction LTV</div>

      $fret_chk->execute([$cid]);
      if ((int)$fret_chk->fetchColumn() > 0) $sig_r[] = ['label'=>'Facture en retard >7j','color'=>'var(--red)'];

    </div>

<script>
function validerSeuils() {
  const seuils = {
    ltv_cac_min: parseFloat(document.getElementById('s_ltv_cac').value),
    taux_conversion_min: parseFloat(document.getElementById('s_taux').value),
    cac_max: parseInt(document.getElementById('s_cac').value),
    budget_pub_max: parseInt(document.getElementById('s_budget').value)
  };
  fetch('alertes.php?action=sauvegarder_seuils&candidat_id=<?= $cid ?>', {
    method: 'POST',
    credentials: 'same-origin',
    headers: {'Content-Type': 'application/json'},
    body: JSON.stringify(seuils)
  }).then(r => r.json()).then(d => {
    if (d.success) { location.reload(); }
  });
}

function regenererSeuils() {
  document.getElementById('seuilsLoader').style.display = 'block';
  fetch('alertes.php?action=proposer_seuils&candidat_id=<?= $cid ?>', {credentials: 'same-origin'})
    .then(r => r.json())
    .then(d => {
      document.getElementById('seuilsLoader').style.display = 'none';
      if (d.ltv_cac_min) {
        // Afficher formulaire inline
        const html = `<div class="card" style="border-color:rgba(201,169,110,.4);margin-top:1rem">
          <div class="sub-label" style="color:#c9a96e"> Nouveaux seuils proposs</div>
          <p style="font-size:.82rem;color:#b0aaa0;margin-bottom:1rem;font-style:italic">${d.justification || ''}</p>
          <div class="grid2">
            <div class="form-row"><label>LTV:CAC minimum</label><input type="number" id="s_ltv_cac" step="0.1" value="${d.ltv_cac_min}"/></div>
            <div class="form-row"><label>Taux conversion min (%)</label><input type="number" id="s_taux" step="0.1" value="${d.taux_conversion_min}"/></div>
            <div class="form-row"><label>CAC max (FCFA)</label><input type="number" id="s_cac" value="${d.cac_max}"/></div>
            <div class="form-row"><label>Budget pub max (FCFA)</label><input type="number" id="s_budget" value="${d.budget_pub_max}"/></div>
          </div>
          <button onclick="validerSeuils()" class="btn btn-gold" style="margin-top:.5rem">Valider</button>
        </div>`;
        document.getElementById('seuilsLoader').insertAdjacentHTML('afterend', html);
      }
    });
}

function lireAlerte(id) {
  fetch('alertes.php?action=lire_alerte&alerte_id=' + id + '&candidat_id=<?= $cid ?>', {credentials: 'same-origin'})
    .then(() => { document.getElementById('alerte-' + id).style.opacity = '.5'; });
}

function lireToutesAlertes() {
  fetch('alertes.php?action=lire_toutes&candidat_id=<?= $cid ?>', {credentials: 'same-origin'})
    .then(() => location.reload());
}
</script>

<script>
function saveTracking(){
  const data=new FormData(document.getElementById('formTracking'));
  fetch('tracking.php',{method:'POST',body:data,credentials:'same-origin'}).then(r=>r.json()).then(d=>{
    if(d.success){const b=document.querySelector('button[onclick="saveTracking()"]');b.textContent=' Sauvegard';b.style.background='#6fcf8a';setTimeout(()=>{b.textContent='Sauvegarder';b.style.background='';},2000);}
  });
}
function loadTracking(){
  document.getElementById('trackingLoader').style.display='block';
  document.getElementById('trackingDashboard').style.display='none';
  fetch('tracking.php?action=fetch&candidat_id=<?= $cid ?>',{credentials:'same-origin'}).then(r=>r.json()).then(d=>{
    document.getElementById('trackingLoader').style.display='none';
    document.getElementById('trackingDashboard').style.display='block';
    if(d.error){document.getElementById('trackingContent').innerHTML='<p style="color:var(--red);padding:1rem">'+d.error+'</p>';return;}
    renderTracking(d);
  }).catch(()=>{document.getElementById('trackingLoader').style.display='none';document.getElementById('trackingContent').innerHTML='<p style="color:var(--red);padding:1rem">Erreur connexion.</p>';document.getElementById('trackingDashboard').style.display='block';});
}
function fmt(n){return Number(n).toLocaleString('fr-FR');}
function kpiBox(label,val,color){const c=color||'var(--gold)';return '<div style="background:#0a0a0e;border:1px solid var(--border);border-radius:12px;padding:.9rem;text-align:center"><div style="font-family:Georgia,serif;font-size:1.4rem;font-weight:700;color:'+c+';line-height:1">'+val+'</div><div style="font-size:.7rem;color:var(--muted);text-transform:uppercase;letter-spacing:.08em;margin-top:.25rem">'+label+'</div></div>';}
function renderTracking(d){
  let html='<p style="font-size:.75rem;color:var(--muted);margin-bottom:1rem">Mise  jour : '+d.date+'</p>';
  if(d.ga4&&d.ga4.totaux&&!d.ga4.error){
    const t=d.ga4.totaux;
    html+='<div style="margin-bottom:1.5rem"><div style="font-size:.72rem;text-transform:uppercase;letter-spacing:.12em;color:var(--muted);margin-bottom:.8rem">Google Analytics 4  30 jours</div>';
    html+='<div style="display:grid;grid-template-columns:repeat(3,1fr);gap:.7rem">';
    html+=kpiBox('Sessions',fmt(t.sessions))+kpiBox('Utilisateurs',fmt(t.utilisateurs))+kpiBox('Nouveaux',fmt(t.nouveaux));
    html+=kpiBox('Taux rebond',t.taux_rebond+'%')+kpiBox('Dure moy.',Math.floor(t.duree_moy/60)+'min'+(t.duree_moy%60)+'s')+kpiBox('Conversions',fmt(t.conversions));
    html+='</div>';
    if(d.ga4.par_canal&&d.ga4.par_canal.length>0){
      html+='<div style="margin-top:.8rem;background:#0a0a0e;border:1px solid var(--border);border-radius:12px;overflow:hidden"><div class="table-wrap"><table style="width:100%;border-collapse:collapse"><thead><tr>';
      ['Canal','Sessions','Utilisateurs','Conv.'].forEach(h=>{html+='<th style="font-size:.7rem;text-transform:uppercase;color:var(--muted);padding:.55rem .8rem;text-align:left;border-bottom:1px solid var(--border)">'+h+'</th>';});
      html+='</tr></thead><tbody>';
      d.ga4.par_canal.forEach(c=>{html+='<tr><td style="padding:.55rem .8rem;font-size:.85rem">'+c.canal+'</td><td style="padding:.55rem .8rem;font-size:.85rem">'+fmt(c.sessions)+'</td><td style="padding:.55rem .8rem;font-size:.85rem">'+fmt(c.utilisateurs)+'</td><td style="padding:.55rem .8rem;font-size:.85rem;color:var(--green)">'+c.conversions+'</td></tr>';});
      html+='</tbody></table></div></div>';
    }
    html+='</div>';
  } else if(d.ga4&&d.ga4.error){html+='<div style="background:rgba(224,112,112,.08);border:1px solid rgba(224,112,112,.2);border-radius:12px;padding:1rem;color:var(--red);font-size:.85rem;margin-bottom:1rem">GA4 : '+d.ga4.error+'</div>';}
  if(d.search_console&&d.search_console.totaux&&!d.search_console.error){
    const t=d.search_console.totaux;
    html+='<div style="margin-bottom:1.5rem"><div style="font-size:.72rem;text-transform:uppercase;letter-spacing:.12em;color:var(--muted);margin-bottom:.8rem">Search Console  30 jours</div>';
    html+='<div style="display:grid;grid-template-columns:repeat(4,1fr);gap:.7rem">';
    html+=kpiBox('Clics',fmt(t.clics))+kpiBox('Impressions',fmt(t.impressions))+kpiBox('CTR',t.ctr_moy+'%')+kpiBox('Position moy.',t.position_moy);
    html+='</div>';
    if(d.search_console.mots_cles&&d.search_console.mots_cles.length>0){
      html+='<div style="margin-top:.8rem;background:#0a0a0e;border:1px solid var(--border);border-radius:12px;overflow:hidden"><div class="table-wrap"><table style="width:100%;border-collapse:collapse"><thead><tr>';
      ['Mot-cl','Clics','Impressions','CTR','Position'].forEach(h=>{html+='<th style="font-size:.7rem;text-transform:uppercase;color:var(--muted);padding:.55rem .8rem;text-align:left;border-bottom:1px solid var(--border)">'+h+'</th>';});
      html+='</tr></thead><tbody>';
      d.search_console.mots_cles.forEach(k=>{html+='<tr><td style="padding:.55rem .8rem;font-size:.82rem;color:var(--gold)">'+k.mot_cle+'</td><td style="padding:.55rem .8rem;font-size:.82rem">'+k.clics+'</td><td style="padding:.55rem .8rem;font-size:.82rem">'+fmt(k.impressions)+'</td><td style="padding:.55rem .8rem;font-size:.82rem">'+k.ctr+'%</td><td style="padding:.55rem .8rem;font-size:.82rem">'+k.position+'</td></tr>';});
      html+='</tbody></table></div></div>';
    }
    html+='</div>';
  } else if(d.search_console&&d.search_console.error){html+='<div style="background:rgba(224,112,112,.08);border:1px solid rgba(224,112,112,.2);border-radius:12px;padding:1rem;color:var(--red);font-size:.85rem;margin-bottom:1rem">Search Console : '+d.search_console.error+'</div>';}
  if(d.meta&&!d.meta.error){
    const m=d.meta;
    html+='<div style="margin-bottom:1.5rem"><div style="font-size:.72rem;text-transform:uppercase;letter-spacing:.12em;color:var(--muted);margin-bottom:.8rem">Meta Ads  30 jours</div>';
    html+='<div style="display:grid;grid-template-columns:repeat(4,1fr);gap:.7rem">';
    html+=kpiBox('Dpenses',fmt(m.depenses)+' FCFA')+kpiBox('Impressions',fmt(m.impressions))+kpiBox('Clics',fmt(m.clics))+kpiBox('Conversions',m.conversions,m.conversions>0?'#6fcf8a':null);
    html+=kpiBox('CPM',fmt(m.cpm)+' FCFA')+kpiBox('CPC',fmt(m.cpc)+' FCFA')+kpiBox('CTR',m.ctr+'%');
    html+='</div></div>';
  } else if(d.meta&&d.meta.error){html+='<div style="background:rgba(224,112,112,.08);border:1px solid rgba(224,112,112,.2);border-radius:12px;padding:1rem;color:var(--red);font-size:.85rem;margin-bottom:1rem">Meta Ads : '+d.meta.error+'</div>';}
  document.getElementById('trackingContent').innerHTML=html;
}
</script>

// ============================================================
// ACTIONS POST  MODULE FORMATION
// ============================================================
if ($_SERVER['REQUEST_METHOD'] === 'POST' && in_array($_POST['action'] ?? '', [
    'confirmer_inscription','annuler_inscription','relance_formation',
    'sauvegarder_paiement_formation','sauvegarder_session',
    'toggle_sequence','sauvegarder_template_sequence'
])) {
    $act_fm = $_POST['action'];
    $fid    = (int)($_POST['inscrit_id'] ?? 0);

    if ($act_fm === 'confirmer_inscription') {
        $date1 = trim($_POST['date_session1'] ?? '');
        $lien1 = trim($_POST['lien_visio1'] ?? '');
        $type1 = trim($_POST['formation_type1'] ?? '');
        $date2 = trim($_POST['date_session2'] ?? '');
        $lien2 = trim($_POST['lien_visio2'] ?? '');
        $type2 = trim($_POST['formation_type2'] ?? '');
        $fi = $pdo->prepare("SELECT * FROM formation_inscrits WHERE id=?");
        $fi->execute([$fid]);
        $fi = $fi->fetch();
        if (!$fi) { header('Location: admin.php?page=formation&msg=err'); exit; }
        $mdp_clair = '';
        if (!$fi['compte_active']) {
            $mdp_clair = substr(str_shuffle('abcdefghjkmnpqrstuvwxyz23456789'), 0, 8);
            $hash_fm   = password_hash($mdp_clair, PASSWORD_DEFAULT);
            $pdo->prepare("UPDATE formation_inscrits SET mot_de_passe=?,compte_active=1,statut='session_planifiee',date_session1=?,lien_visio1=?,formation_type1=?,date_session2=?,lien_visio2=?,formation_type2=?,confirmation_at=NOW(),updated_at=NOW() WHERE id=?")
                ->execute([$hash_fm,$date1?:null,$lien1?:null,$type1?:null,$date2?:null,$lien2?:null,$type2?:null,$fid]);
        } else {
            $pdo->prepare("UPDATE formation_inscrits SET statut='session_planifiee',date_session1=?,lien_visio1=?,formation_type1=?,date_session2=?,lien_visio2=?,formation_type2=?,updated_at=NOW() WHERE id=?")
                ->execute([$date1?:null,$lien1?:null,$type1?:null,$date2?:null,$lien2?:null,$type2?:null,$fid]);
        }
        if ($date1 && $lien1) {
            $date_fmt = date('d/m/Y  H:i', strtotime($date1));
            sendConfirmationFormation($fi['email'],$fi['nom'],$fi['formation']??'Formation ePerformance',$date_fmt,$lien1,$mdp_clair);
        }
        sendTelegram(" <b>Inscription confirme</b>\n " . $fi['nom'] . "\n " . ($fi['formation']??'') . "\n " . ($date1 ? date('d/m/Y H:i',strtotime($date1)) : ' planifier'));
        header('Location: admin.php?page=formation&id=' . $fid . '&msg=confirme');
        exit;
    }

    if ($act_fm === 'annuler_inscription') {
        $pdo->prepare("UPDATE formation_inscrits SET statut='annule',updated_at=NOW() WHERE id=?")->execute([$fid]);
        header('Location: admin.php?page=formation&msg=annule');
        exit;
    }

    if ($act_fm === 'relance_formation') {
        $fi_r = $pdo->prepare("SELECT * FROM formation_inscrits WHERE id=?");
        $fi_r->execute([$fid]);
        $fi_r = $fi_r->fetch();
        if ($fi_r) {
            $html_rel = '<!DOCTYPE html><html><body style="background:#08080c;color:#edeae3;font-family:Arial,sans-serif;padding:32px"><div style="max-width:540px;margin:0 auto;background:#101014;border:1px solid #1c1c22;border-radius:16px;padding:28px"><div style="font-family:Georgia,serif;font-size:24px;color:#c9a96e;margin-bottom:20px">ePerformance</div><p>Bonjour ' . htmlspecialchars($fi_r['nom']) . ',</p><p style="color:#b0aaa0;line-height:1.7;margin:16px 0">Suite  votre demande d&#39;inscription, je reviens vers vous pour confirmer votre place.</p><p style="color:#b0aaa0;line-height:1.7">Si vous souhaitez toujours vous inscrire, rpondez  cet email ou contactez-moi directement.</p><p style="margin-top:24px;font-size:13px;color:#7a7a85">K. Stphane  ePerformance</p></div></body></html>';
            sendBrevo($fi_r['email'], $fi_r['nom'], 'Suite  votre demande  ePerformance Formation', $html_rel);
            $pdo->prepare("UPDATE formation_inscrits SET relance_at=NOW(),statut='contacte',updated_at=NOW() WHERE id=?")->execute([$fid]);
        }
        header('Location: admin.php?page=formation&id=' . $fid . '&msg=relance_ok');
        exit;
    }

    if ($act_fm === 'sauvegarder_paiement_formation') {
        $montant_fm = (float)($_POST['montant'] ?? 0);
        $mode_fm    = $_POST['mode_paiement'] ?? 'autre';
        $date_fm    = $_POST['date_paiement'] ?? date('Y-m-d');
        $ref_fm     = trim($_POST['ref_paiement'] ?? '');
        $pdo->prepare("UPDATE formation_inscrits SET montant=?,mode_paiement=?,date_paiement=?,ref_paiement=?,statut='confirme',updated_at=NOW() WHERE id=?")
            ->execute([$montant_fm,$mode_fm,$date_fm,$ref_fm,$fid]);
        $fi_pay = $pdo->prepare("SELECT * FROM formation_inscrits WHERE id=?");
        $fi_pay->execute([$fid]);
        $fi_pay = $fi_pay->fetch();
        sendTelegram(" <b>Paiement formation</b>\n " . ($fi_pay['nom']??'') . "\n " . number_format($montant_fm,0,',',' ') . " FCFA\n " . $mode_fm);
        header('Location: admin.php?page=formation&id=' . $fid . '&msg=paiement_ok');
        exit;
    }

    if ($act_fm === 'sauvegarder_session') {
        $notes_fm = trim($_POST['notes_admin'] ?? '');
        $pdo->prepare("UPDATE formation_inscrits SET statut='termine',notes_admin=?,updated_at=NOW() WHERE id=?")->execute([$notes_fm,$fid]);
        header('Location: admin.php?page=formation&id=' . $fid . '&msg=termine');
        exit;
    }

    if ($act_fm === 'toggle_sequence') {
        $seq_id = (int)($_POST['sequence_id'] ?? 0);
        $pdo->prepare("UPDATE email_sequences SET actif=1-actif,updated_at=NOW() WHERE id=?")->execute([$seq_id]);
        header('Location: admin.php?page=sequences&msg=ok');
        exit;
    }

    if ($act_fm === 'sauvegarder_template_sequence') {
        $seq_id_t = (int)($_POST['sequence_id'] ?? 0);
        $sujet_t  = trim($_POST['sujet'] ?? '');
        $html_t   = trim($_POST['contenu_html'] ?? '');
        $pdo->prepare("UPDATE email_sequences SET sujet=?,contenu_html=?,updated_at=NOW() WHERE id=?")->execute([$sujet_t,$html_t,$seq_id_t]);
        header('Location: admin.php?page=sequences&msg=sauvegarde');
        exit;
    }
}




// ============================================================
// ACTIONS POST  MODULE COMPTABILIT
// ============================================================
if ($_SERVER['REQUEST_METHOD'] === 'POST' && in_array($_POST['action'] ?? '', [
    'ajouter_revenu_manuel','ajouter_depense','supprimer_depense','sauvegarder_charge_fixe','reporter_charges'
])) {
    $act_co = $_POST['action'];

    if ($act_co === 'ajouter_revenu_manuel') {
        $rm_mois    = $_POST['mois_revenu'] ?? date('Y-m');
        $rm_libelle = trim($_POST['libelle_revenu'] ?? '');
        $rm_montant = (int)($_POST['montant_revenu'] ?? 0);
        $rm_client  = trim($_POST['client_nom_revenu'] ?? '');
        $rm_cat     = trim($_POST['categorie_revenu'] ?? 'Autre');
        $rm_date    = $_POST['date_paiement_revenu'] ?? date('Y-m-d');
        $rm_ref     = trim($_POST['reference_revenu'] ?? '');
        if ($rm_libelle && $rm_montant > 0) {
            $pdo->prepare("INSERT INTO comptabilite_revenus_manuels (mois, libelle, categorie, montant, client_nom, reference, date_paiement, created_at) VALUES (?,?,?,?,?,?,?,NOW())")
                ->execute([$rm_mois, $rm_libelle, $rm_cat, $rm_montant, $rm_client, $rm_ref, $rm_date]);
        }
        header('Location: admin.php?page=comptabilite&mois=' . $rm_mois . '&msg=revenu_manuel_ok');
        exit;
    }

    if ($act_co === 'ajouter_depense') {
        $mois_co   = trim($_POST['mois'] ?? date('Y-m'));
        $cat_co    = trim($_POST['categorie'] ?? 'divers');
        $lib_co    = trim($_POST['libelle'] ?? '');
        $mont_co   = (int)preg_replace('/[^0-9]/', '', $_POST['montant'] ?? '0');
        $rec_co    = isset($_POST['recurrente']) ? 1 : 0;
        if ($lib_co && $mont_co > 0) {
            $pdo->prepare("INSERT INTO comptabilite_depenses (mois, categorie, libelle, montant, recurrente, created_at) VALUES (?,?,?,?,?,NOW())")
                ->execute([$mois_co, $cat_co, $lib_co, $mont_co, $rec_co]);
        }
        header('Location: admin.php?page=comptabilite&mois=' . $mois_co . '&msg=depense_ok');
        exit;
    }

    if ($act_co === 'supprimer_depense') {
        $dep_id = (int)$_POST['depense_id'];
        $pdo->prepare("DELETE FROM comptabilite_depenses WHERE id=?")->execute([$dep_id]);
        header('Location: ' . ($_SERVER['HTTP_REFERER'] ?? 'admin.php?page=comptabilite'));
        exit;
    }

    if ($act_co === 'sauvegarder_charge_fixe') {
        $cf_id   = (int)$_POST['charge_id'];
        $cf_mont = (int)preg_replace('/[^0-9]/', '', $_POST['montant'] ?? '0');
        $cf_actif = isset($_POST['actif']) ? 1 : 0;
        $pdo->prepare("UPDATE comptabilite_charges_fixes SET montant=?, actif=?, updated_at=NOW() WHERE id=?")
            ->execute([$cf_mont, $cf_actif, $cf_id]);
        header('Location: admin.php?page=comptabilite&tab=charges&msg=charge_ok');
        exit;
    }

    if ($act_co === 'reporter_charges') {
        $mois_co = trim($_POST['mois'] ?? date('Y-m'));
        $charges = $pdo->query("SELECT * FROM comptabilite_charges_fixes WHERE actif=1")->fetchAll();
        $ok = 0;
        foreach ($charges as $ch) {
            $exists = $pdo->prepare("SELECT id FROM comptabilite_depenses WHERE mois=? AND categorie=? AND libelle=? AND recurrente=1");
            $exists->execute([$mois_co, $ch['categorie'], $ch['libelle']]);
            if (!$exists->fetch()) {
                $pdo->prepare("INSERT INTO comptabilite_depenses (mois, categorie, libelle, montant, recurrente, created_at) VALUES (?,?,?,?,1,NOW())")
                    ->execute([$mois_co, $ch['categorie'], $ch['libelle'], $ch['montant']]);
                $ok++;
            }
        }
        header('Location: admin.php?page=comptabilite&mois=' . $mois_co . '&msg=charges_reportees&nb=' . $ok);
        exit;
    }
}



// ============================================================
// EXPORT CSV  COMPTABILIT
// ============================================================
if ($page === 'comptabilite' && isset($_GET['export']) && $_GET['export'] === 'csv') {
    $mois_exp = $_GET['mois'] ?? date('Y-m');

    // Revenus toutes sources
    $encaiss_acc_exp = $pdo->prepare("SELECT COALESCE(SUM(montant),0) FROM factures WHERE statut='payee' AND DATE_FORMAT(date_paiement,'%Y-%m')=?");
    $encaiss_acc_exp->execute([$mois_exp]);
    $encaiss_web_exp = $pdo->prepare("SELECT COALESCE(SUM(montant),0) FROM clients_web_factures WHERE statut='payee' AND DATE_FORMAT(date_paiement,'%Y-%m')=?");
    $encaiss_web_exp->execute([$mois_exp]);
    $encaiss_form_exp = $pdo->prepare("SELECT COALESCE(SUM(montant),0) FROM formation_inscrits WHERE statut='confirme' AND DATE_FORMAT(date_paiement,'%Y-%m')=?");
    $encaiss_form_exp->execute([$mois_exp]);
    $encaiss_man_exp = $pdo->prepare("SELECT COALESCE(SUM(montant),0) FROM comptabilite_revenus_manuels WHERE mois=?");
    $encaiss_man_exp->execute([$mois_exp]);
    $total_enc_exp = (int)$encaiss_acc_exp->fetchColumn() + (int)$encaiss_web_exp->fetchColumn() + (int)$encaiss_form_exp->fetchColumn() + (int)$encaiss_man_exp->fetchColumn();

    // Dtail factures toutes sources pour export
    $factures_exp_all = [];
    $fa_e1 = $pdo->prepare("SELECT f.reference, f.montant, f.date_paiement as date_emission, c.nom, 'Accompagnement' as source FROM factures f LEFT JOIN candidats c ON c.id=f.candidat_id WHERE f.statut='payee' AND DATE_FORMAT(f.date_paiement,'%Y-%m')=?");
    $fa_e1->execute([$mois_exp]); foreach($fa_e1->fetchAll() as $r) $factures_exp_all[] = $r;
    $fa_e2 = $pdo->prepare("SELECT f.reference, f.montant, f.date_paiement as date_emission, c.nom, 'Clients Web' as source FROM clients_web_factures f LEFT JOIN clients_web c ON c.id=f.client_id WHERE f.statut='payee' AND DATE_FORMAT(f.date_paiement,'%Y-%m')=?");
    $fa_e2->execute([$mois_exp]); foreach($fa_e2->fetchAll() as $r) $factures_exp_all[] = $r;
    $fa_e3 = $pdo->prepare("SELECT CONCAT('FO-',id) as reference, montant, date_paiement as date_emission, nom, 'Formation' as source FROM formation_inscrits WHERE statut='confirme' AND DATE_FORMAT(date_paiement,'%Y-%m')=?");
    $fa_e3->execute([$mois_exp]); foreach($fa_e3->fetchAll() as $r) $factures_exp_all[] = $r;
    $fa_e4 = $pdo->prepare("SELECT reference, montant, date_paiement as date_emission, client_nom as nom, categorie as source FROM comptabilite_revenus_manuels WHERE mois=?");
    $fa_e4->execute([$mois_exp]); foreach($fa_e4->fetchAll() as $r) $factures_exp_all[] = $r;

    $depenses_exp = $pdo->prepare("SELECT * FROM comptabilite_depenses WHERE mois=? ORDER BY categorie, libelle");
    $depenses_exp->execute([$mois_exp]);
    $depenses_exp = $depenses_exp->fetchAll();
    $total_dep_exp = array_sum(array_column($depenses_exp, 'montant'));

    $filename = 'comptabilite_eperformance_' . $mois_exp . '.csv';
    header('Content-Type: text/csv; charset=utf-8');
    header('Content-Disposition: attachment; filename="' . $filename . '"');
    header('Pragma: no-cache');

    $out = fopen('php://output', 'w');
    fprintf($out, chr(0xEF).chr(0xBB).chr(0xBF)); // BOM UTF-8

    // En-tte
    fputcsv($out, ['ePerformance  Comptabilit ' . $mois_exp], ';');
    fputcsv($out, [], ';');

    // Encaissements
    fputcsv($out, ['ENCAISSEMENTS'], ';');
    fputcsv($out, ['Rfrence', 'Client', 'Source', 'Date', 'Montant (FCFA)'], ';');
    foreach ($factures_exp_all as $f_exp) {
        fputcsv($out, [
            $f_exp['reference'] ?? '',
            $f_exp['nom'] ?? '',
            $f_exp['source'] ?? '',
            !empty($f_exp['date_emission']) ? date('d/m/Y', strtotime($f_exp['date_emission'])) : '',
            $f_exp['montant'],
        ], ';');
    }
    fputcsv($out, ['', '', 'TOTAL ENCAISSEMENTS', $total_enc_exp], ';');
    fputcsv($out, [], ';');

    // Dpenses
    fputcsv($out, ['DPENSES'], ';');
    fputcsv($out, ['Catgorie', 'Libell', 'Rcurrente', 'Montant (FCFA)'], ';');
    $cats_exp = ['lws'=>'LWS','anthropic'=>'Anthropic','brevo'=>'Brevo','whatsapp'=>'WhatsApp','publicite'=>'Publicit','outils'=>'Outils','frais_bancaires'=>'Frais bancaires','divers'=>'Divers'];
    foreach ($depenses_exp as $d_exp) {
        fputcsv($out, [
            $cats_exp[$d_exp['categorie']] ?? $d_exp['categorie'],
            $d_exp['libelle'],
            $d_exp['recurrente'] ? 'Oui' : 'Non',
            $d_exp['montant'],
        ], ';');
    }
    fputcsv($out, ['', 'TOTAL DPENSES', '', $total_dep_exp], ';');
    fputcsv($out, [], ';');

    // Rsultat
    fputcsv($out, ['RSULTAT NET', '', '', ($total_enc_exp - $total_dep_exp)], ';');
    $marge = $total_enc_exp > 0 ? round(($total_enc_exp - $total_dep_exp) / $total_enc_exp * 100) : 0;
    fputcsv($out, ['MARGE %', '', '', $marge . '%'], ';');

    fclose($out);
    exit;
}

// ============================================================
// PAGE COMPTABILIT
// ============================================================
if ($page === 'comptabilite') {
    $mois_actuel = $_GET['mois'] ?? date('Y-m');
    $tab_co      = $_GET['tab'] ?? 'tableau';
    $msg_co      = $_GET['msg'] ?? '';

    //  Calcul encaissements du mois depuis factures payes 
    // Sources de revenus unifiees
    $enc_accomp = $pdo->prepare("SELECT COALESCE(SUM(montant),0) FROM factures WHERE statut='payee' AND DATE_FORMAT(date_paiement,'%Y-%m')=?");
    $enc_accomp->execute([$mois_actuel]);
    $total_accomp = (int)$enc_accomp->fetchColumn();
    $enc_web_q = $pdo->prepare("SELECT COALESCE(SUM(montant),0) FROM clients_web_factures WHERE statut='payee' AND DATE_FORMAT(date_paiement,'%Y-%m')=?");
    $enc_web_q->execute([$mois_actuel]);
    $total_web_co = (int)$enc_web_q->fetchColumn();
    $enc_form_q = $pdo->prepare("SELECT COALESCE(SUM(montant),0) FROM formation_inscrits WHERE statut='confirme' AND DATE_FORMAT(date_paiement,'%Y-%m')=?");
    $enc_form_q->execute([$mois_actuel]);
    $total_form_co = (int)$enc_form_q->fetchColumn();
    $enc_man_q = $pdo->prepare("SELECT COALESCE(SUM(montant),0) FROM comptabilite_revenus_manuels WHERE mois=? ");
    $enc_man_q->execute([$mois_actuel]);
    $total_man_co = (int)$enc_man_q->fetchColumn();
    $total_encaiss = $total_accomp + $total_web_co + $total_form_co + $total_man_co;
    $enc_detail = [
        ['type' => 'Accompagnement', 'total' => $total_accomp],
        ['type' => 'Clients Web',    'total' => $total_web_co],
        ['type' => 'Formation',      'total' => $total_form_co],
        ['type' => 'Manuel',         'total' => $total_man_co],
    ];

    //  Dtail encaissements par type 


    //  Dpenses du mois 
    $depenses = $pdo->prepare("SELECT * FROM comptabilite_depenses WHERE mois=? ORDER BY created_at DESC");
    $depenses->execute([$mois_actuel]);
    $depenses = $depenses->fetchAll();
    $total_depenses = array_sum(array_column($depenses, 'montant'));

    //  Rsultat 
    $resultat_net = $total_encaiss - $total_depenses;
    $marge_pct    = $total_encaiss > 0 ? round($resultat_net / $total_encaiss * 100) : 0;

    //  Charges fixes 
    $charges_fixes = $pdo->query("SELECT * FROM comptabilite_charges_fixes ORDER BY actif DESC, categorie")->fetchAll();
    $total_charges_fixes = array_sum(array_column(array_filter($charges_fixes, fn($c) => $c['actif']), 'montant'));

    //  MRR  revenus rcurrents confirms 
    $mrr = $pdo->query("SELECT COALESCE(SUM(montant),0) FROM factures WHERE statut='payee' AND DATE_FORMAT(date_paiement,'%Y-%m')=DATE_FORMAT(NOW(),'%Y-%m')")->fetchColumn();
    $mrr_web = $pdo->query("SELECT COALESCE(SUM(montant),0) FROM clients_web_factures WHERE statut='payee' AND DATE_FORMAT(date_paiement,'%Y-%m')=DATE_FORMAT(NOW(),'%Y-%m')")->fetchColumn();
    $mrr_form = $pdo->query("SELECT COALESCE(SUM(montant),0) FROM formation_inscrits WHERE statut='confirme' AND DATE_FORMAT(date_paiement,'%Y-%m')=DATE_FORMAT(NOW(),'%Y-%m')")->fetchColumn();
    $mrr_total = (int)$mrr + (int)$mrr_web + (int)$mrr_form;

    //  Seuil de rentabilit 
    $panier_moyen = $pdo->query("SELECT COALESCE(AVG(montant),0) FROM factures WHERE statut='payee'")->fetchColumn();
    $seuil_clients = $total_charges_fixes > 0 && $panier_moyen > 0 ? ceil($total_charges_fixes / $panier_moyen) : 0;
    $seuil_atteint = $total_encaiss >= $total_charges_fixes;

    //  Vue annuelle 
    $annee = substr($mois_actuel, 0, 4);
    $ca_acc_an = $pdo->prepare("SELECT COALESCE(SUM(montant),0) FROM factures WHERE statut='payee' AND YEAR(date_paiement)=?");
    $ca_acc_an->execute([$annee]);
    $ca_web_an = $pdo->prepare("SELECT COALESCE(SUM(montant),0) FROM clients_web_factures WHERE statut='payee' AND YEAR(date_paiement)=?");
    $ca_web_an->execute([$annee]);
    $ca_form_an = $pdo->prepare("SELECT COALESCE(SUM(montant),0) FROM formation_inscrits WHERE statut='confirme' AND YEAR(date_paiement)=?");
    $ca_form_an->execute([$annee]);
    $ca_man_an = $pdo->prepare("SELECT COALESCE(SUM(montant),0) FROM comptabilite_revenus_manuels WHERE mois LIKE ?");
    $ca_man_an->execute([$annee.'-%']);
    $ca_annuel = (int)$ca_acc_an->fetchColumn() + (int)$ca_web_an->fetchColumn() + (int)$ca_form_an->fetchColumn() + (int)$ca_man_an->fetchColumn();

    $dep_annuel = $pdo->prepare("SELECT COALESCE(SUM(montant),0) FROM comptabilite_depenses WHERE mois LIKE ?");
    $dep_annuel->execute([$annee . '-%']);
    $dep_annuel = (int)$dep_annuel->fetchColumn();

    $resultat_annuel = $ca_annuel - $dep_annuel;

    //  Taux de conversion 
    $nb_diag = $pdo->query("SELECT COUNT(*) FROM candidats")->fetchColumn();
    $nb_clients = $pdo->query("SELECT COUNT(*) FROM candidats WHERE compte_active=1")->fetchColumn();
    $taux_conv = $nb_diag > 0 ? round($nb_clients / $nb_diag * 100, 1) : 0;

    //  Valeur totale par client 
    $valeur_clients = $pdo->query("SELECT c.nom, COALESCE(SUM(f.montant),0) as total FROM candidats c LEFT JOIN factures f ON f.candidat_id=c.id AND f.statut='payee' GROUP BY c.id, c.nom ORDER BY total DESC LIMIT 10")->fetchAll();

    //  Mois prcdent pour comparaison 
    $mois_prec = date('Y-m', strtotime($mois_actuel . '-01 -1 month'));
    $enc_prec = $pdo->prepare("SELECT COALESCE(SUM(montant),0) FROM factures WHERE statut='payee' AND DATE_FORMAT(date_emission,'%Y-%m')=?");
    $enc_prec->execute([$mois_prec]);
    $enc_prec = (int)$enc_prec->fetchColumn();
    $evolution_enc = $enc_prec > 0 ? round(($total_encaiss - $enc_prec) / $enc_prec * 100) : 0;

    //  Alerte trsorerie 
    $alerte_tresorerie = $total_encaiss < $total_charges_fixes;

    adminHeader('Comptabilit');
    echo '<div class="content">';

    $flash_co = [
        'depense_ok'        => ['ok', 'Dpense enregistre.'],
        'charge_ok'         => ['ok', 'Charge fixe mise  jour.'],
        'charges_reportees' => ['ok', ($_GET['nb'] ?? 0) . ' charge(s) reporte(s) pour ce mois.'],
        'revenu_manuel_ok'  => ['ok', 'Revenu manuel enregistr.'],
    ];
    if ($msg_co && isset($flash_co[$msg_co])) echo '<div class="flash ' . $flash_co[$msg_co][0] . '">' . $flash_co[$msg_co][1] . '</div>';

    //  ALERTE TRSORERIE 
    if ($alerte_tresorerie && $total_charges_fixes > 0): ?>
    <div style="background:rgba(248,113,113,.08);border:1px solid rgba(248,113,113,.3);border-radius:14px;padding:1rem 1.4rem;display:flex;align-items:center;gap:.8rem;margin-bottom:1.5rem">
      <i class="fa-solid fa-triangle-exclamation" style="color:#f87171;font-size:1.1rem"></i>
      <div style="font-size:.88rem;color:#f87171">
        <strong>Alerte trsorerie</strong>  Vos encaissements ce mois (<?= number_format($total_encaiss,0,',',' ') ?> FCFA) ne couvrent pas encore vos charges fixes (<?= number_format($total_charges_fixes,0,',',' ') ?> FCFA).
      </div>
    </div>
    <?php endif; ?>

    <div class="page-header">
      <div>
        <h1 style="font-family:'Cormorant Garamond',serif;font-size:1.9rem;font-weight:700">Comptabilit</h1>
        <p style="color:var(--muted);font-size:.88rem;margin-top:.3rem">Suivi financier ePerformance</p>
      </div>
      <div style="display:flex;align-items:center;gap:.7rem;flex-wrap:wrap">
        <input type="month" value="<?= $mois_actuel ?>" onchange="location.href='?page=comptabilite&mois='+this.value" class="field-input" style="width:auto;padding:.4rem .8rem"/>
        <a href="?page=comptabilite&tab=charges" class="btn btn-outline btn-sm"> Charges fixes</a>
        <a href="?page=comptabilite&export=csv&mois=<?= $mois_actuel ?>" class="btn btn-outline btn-sm"> Export CSV</a>
      </div>
    </div>

    <!-- CARDS KPIs -->
    <div style="display:grid;grid-template-columns:repeat(auto-fit,minmax(200px,1fr));gap:1rem;margin-bottom:1.5rem">

      <div class="card" style="text-align:center">
        <div style="font-size:.68rem;text-transform:uppercase;letter-spacing:.12em;color:var(--muted);margin-bottom:.6rem">Encaissements</div>
        <div style="font-family:'Cormorant Garamond',serif;font-size:1.8rem;font-weight:700;color:var(--green)"><?= number_format($total_encaiss,0,',',' ') ?></div>
        <div style="font-size:.72rem;color:var(--muted)">FCFA <?php if ($enc_prec > 0): ?><span style="color:<?= $evolution_enc >= 0 ? 'var(--green)' : 'var(--red)' ?>"><?= ($evolution_enc >= 0 ? '+' : '') . $evolution_enc ?>% vs mois prc.</span><?php endif; ?></div>
      </div>

      <div class="card" style="text-align:center">
        <div style="font-size:.68rem;text-transform:uppercase;letter-spacing:.12em;color:var(--muted);margin-bottom:.6rem">Dpenses</div>
        <div style="font-family:'Cormorant Garamond',serif;font-size:1.8rem;font-weight:700;color:var(--red)"><?= number_format($total_depenses,0,',',' ') ?></div>
        <div style="font-size:.72rem;color:var(--muted)">FCFA ce mois</div>
      </div>

      <div class="card" style="text-align:center">
        <div style="font-size:.68rem;text-transform:uppercase;letter-spacing:.12em;color:var(--muted);margin-bottom:.6rem">Rsultat net</div>
        <div style="font-family:'Cormorant Garamond',serif;font-size:1.8rem;font-weight:700;color:<?= $resultat_net >= 0 ? 'var(--gold)' : 'var(--red)' ?>"><?= ($resultat_net >= 0 ? '+' : '') . number_format($resultat_net,0,',',' ') ?></div>
        <div style="font-size:.72rem;color:var(--muted)">FCFA  Marge <?= $marge_pct ?>%</div>
      </div>

      <div class="card" style="text-align:center">
        <div style="font-size:.68rem;text-transform:uppercase;letter-spacing:.12em;color:var(--muted);margin-bottom:.6rem">MRR</div>
        <div style="font-family:'Cormorant Garamond',serif;font-size:1.8rem;font-weight:700;color:var(--blue)"><?= number_format($mrr_total,0,',',' ') ?></div>
        <div style="font-size:.72rem;color:var(--muted)">FCFA rcurrents confirms</div>
      </div>

      <div class="card" style="text-align:center">
        <div style="font-size:.68rem;text-transform:uppercase;letter-spacing:.12em;color:var(--muted);margin-bottom:.6rem">Seuil rentabilit</div>
        <div style="font-family:'Cormorant Garamond',serif;font-size:1.8rem;font-weight:700;color:<?= $seuil_atteint ? 'var(--green)' : 'var(--gold)' ?>"><?= $seuil_atteint ? ' Atteint' : $seuil_clients . ' clients' ?></div>
        <div style="font-size:.72rem;color:var(--muted)"><?= $seuil_atteint ? 'Charges couvertes' : 'pour couvrir les charges' ?></div>
      </div>

      <div class="card" style="text-align:center">
        <div style="font-size:.68rem;text-transform:uppercase;letter-spacing:.12em;color:var(--muted);margin-bottom:.6rem">Taux de conversion</div>
        <div style="font-family:'Cormorant Garamond',serif;font-size:1.8rem;font-weight:700;color:var(--gold)"><?= $taux_conv ?>%</div>
        <div style="font-size:.72rem;color:var(--muted)">Diagnostic  client actif</div>
      </div>

    </div>

    <!-- VUE ANNUELLE -->
    <div class="card" style="margin-bottom:1.5rem">
      <div style="font-size:.68rem;text-transform:uppercase;letter-spacing:.12em;color:var(--muted);margin-bottom:1rem">Anne <?= $annee ?></div>
      <div style="display:grid;grid-template-columns:repeat(3,1fr);gap:1.5rem;text-align:center">
        <div>
          <div style="font-size:.78rem;color:var(--muted)">CA annuel</div>
          <div style="font-family:'Cormorant Garamond',serif;font-size:1.5rem;font-weight:700;color:var(--green)"><?= number_format($ca_annuel,0,',',' ') ?> FCFA</div>
        </div>
        <div>
          <div style="font-size:.78rem;color:var(--muted)">Dpenses annuelles</div>
          <div style="font-family:'Cormorant Garamond',serif;font-size:1.5rem;font-weight:700;color:var(--red)"><?= number_format($dep_annuel,0,',',' ') ?> FCFA</div>
        </div>
        <div>
          <div style="font-size:.78rem;color:var(--muted)">Rsultat annuel</div>
          <div style="font-family:'Cormorant Garamond',serif;font-size:1.5rem;font-weight:700;color:<?= $resultat_annuel >= 0 ? 'var(--gold)' : 'var(--red)' ?>"><?= ($resultat_annuel >= 0 ? '+' : '') . number_format($resultat_annuel,0,',',' ') ?> FCFA</div>
        </div>
      </div>
    </div>

    <div style="display:grid;grid-template-columns:1fr 1fr;gap:1.2rem;margin-bottom:1.5rem">

      <!-- DPENSES DU MOIS -->
      <div class="card">
        <div style="display:flex;align-items:center;justify-content:space-between;margin-bottom:1rem">
          <span style="font-size:.68rem;text-transform:uppercase;letter-spacing:.12em;color:var(--muted)">Dpenses  <?= date('F Y', strtotime($mois_actuel . '-01')) ?></span>
          <form method="POST" style="margin:0;display:inline">
            <input type="hidden" name="action" value="reporter_charges"/>
            <input type="hidden" name="mois" value="<?= $mois_actuel ?>"/>
            <button type="submit" class="btn-sm btn-outline" style="font-size:.72rem"> Reporter charges fixes</button>
          </form>
        </div>

        <?php if (empty($depenses)): ?>
        <div style="text-align:center;padding:1.5rem;color:var(--muted);font-size:.85rem">Aucune dpense ce mois.</div>
        <?php else: ?>
        <?php

        $html_recon = callClaude($prompt_recon, 2500);
        if (!empty($html_recon)) {
            preg_match('/<html[\s\S]*<\/html>/i', $html_recon, $m);
            if (!empty($m[0])) $html_recon = $m[0];
        }

        $sujet_recon = "Proposition de reconstruction  " . $site . " (" . $chemin_label . ")";
        $pdo->prepare("INSERT INTO clients_web_emails (client_id, type, sujet, contenu_html, statut, created_at) VALUES (?,?,?,?,'brouillon',NOW())")
            ->execute([$cw_id, 'renouvellement', $sujet_recon, $html_recon]);

        sendTelegram(" <b>Proposition reconstruction gnre</b>
 " . $nom . "
 " . $site . "
 Chemin " . $chemin . "  " . $chemin_label);
        header('Location: admin.php?page=clients_web&id=' . $cw_id . '&msg=reconstruction_ok');
        exit;
    }


    if ($act_cw === 'generer_livrables') {
        set_time_limit(600);
        $cw_id  = (int)$_POST['client_id'];
        $chemin = $_POST['chemin'] ?? 'B';
        $cw_l = $pdo->prepare("SELECT * FROM clients_web WHERE id=?"); $cw_l->execute([$cw_id]); $cw_l = $cw_l->fetch();
        if (!$cw_l) { header('Location: admin.php?page=clients_web'); exit; }
        $rapport_l = $pdo->prepare("SELECT * FROM clients_web_rapports WHERE client_id=? ORDER BY created_at DESC LIMIT 1"); $rapport_l->execute([$cw_id]); $rapport_l = $rapport_l->fetch();
        $produits_db = $pdo->prepare("SELECT * FROM clients_web_produits WHERE client_id=? AND actif=1 ORDER BY ordre"); $produits_db->execute([$cw_id]); $produits_db = $produits_db->fetchAll();
        $max_v_q = $pdo->prepare("SELECT COALESCE(MAX(version),0) as max_v FROM clients_web_livrables WHERE client_id=?"); $max_v_q->execute([$cw_id]); $next_version = (int)($max_v_q->fetch()['max_v']) + 1;
        $nom_l  = $cw_l['nom']; $site_l = $cw_l['site_web'] ?? ''; $score_l = $rapport_l ? $rapport_l['score_sante'] : 0;
        $csv_extrait_l = $rapport_l ? mb_substr($rapport_l['csv_data'] ?? '', 0, 2000) : '';
        $code_source = $cw_l['code_source_existant'] ?? ''; $has_code = !empty($code_source);
        $gmb_url = $cw_l['gmb_url'] ?? ''; $gmb_id = $cw_l['gmb_id'] ?? ''; $mc_id = $cw_l['merchant_center_id'] ?? '';
        $whatsapp_num = preg_replace('/\D/', '', $cw_l['telephone'] ?? '225XXXXXXXXXX');

        // Construire le catalogue produits
        $produits_context = '';
        foreach ($produits_db as $pp) {
            $produits_context .= "- NOM:{$pp['nom']} | PRIX:{$pp['prix_unitaire']}FCFA";
            if ($pp['prix_pack2']) $produits_context .= " | PACK2:{$pp['prix_pack2']}FCFA";
            if ($pp['prix_pack8']) $produits_context .= " | PACK8:{$pp['prix_pack8']}FCFA";
            if (!empty($pp['image_url'])) $produits_context .= " | IMG:{$pp['image_url']}";
            if (!empty($pp['description'])) $produits_context .= " | DESC:{$pp['description']}";
            $produits_context .= "\n";
        }

        $ctx_base = "Site: $site_l | Domaine: $site_l | Score SEO: $score_l/100 | $produits_context | Donnees SEO: $csv_extrait_l | GMB: $gmb_url | TG endpoint: https://api.eperformance.pro/commande_telegram.php | TG chat_id: 8441274889 | WhatsApp: $whatsapp_num";
        $style_commun = "Styles OBLIGATOIREMENT inline dans le <style> du <head>. Police: system-ui,sans-serif. Design: fond blanc #fff, vert principal #2A6A3B, texte #333. Mobile-first, responsive. Boutons verts arrondis. Images max-width:100%. Pas de fichier CSS externe.";

        $fichiers_generes = [];

        if ($chemin === 'B') {
            $code_boutique = $has_code ? mb_substr($code_source, 0, 6000) : '';

            //  FICHIER 1 : index.html 
            $p1 = "Genere un fichier index.html COMPLET et AUTONOME pour $site_l. $ctx_base. $style_commun. Contenu: header logo SUPERLIFE OFFICIEL + nav (Accueil|Boutique|Blog|Contact) + hero H1 SEO avec CTA boutique.html + section 3 produits phares avec vraies images IMG du catalogue + section pourquoi choisir (4 avantages) + footer avec liens + Schema.org LocalBusiness. URL canonique: $site_l. Placeholder: <!-- GA4: REMPLACER PAR G-XXXXXXXXXX -->. Retourne UNIQUEMENT le code HTML complet, rien d'autre.";
            $fichiers_generes['index.html'] = callClaude($p1, 5000);

            //  FICHIER 2 : boutique.html 
            $p2_base = "Genere un fichier boutique.html COMPLET et AUTONOME pour $site_l. $ctx_base. $style_commun. ";
