        sendTelegram(" <b>Briefing Ajustements gnr</b>\n $nom\n $site\n $nb2 fichiers, " . count($ajs) . " ajustements");
        header('Location: admin.php?page=clients_web&id=' . $cw_id . '&msg=livrables_ok');
        exit;
    }

}

// ============================================================

// ============================================================
// PAGE CLIENTS WEB
// ============================================================
//  ACTION GET_LIVRABLE  afficher ou tlcharger un livrable ou article 
if (isset($_GET['action']) && $_GET['action'] === 'get_livrable') {
    // Tlcharger un article de blog
    if (!empty($_GET['article_id'])) {
        $art_id = (int)$_GET['article_id'];
        $art = $pdo->prepare("SELECT * FROM clients_web_articles WHERE id=?");
        $art->execute([$art_id]); $art = $art->fetch();
        if ($art) {
            $fname = $art['slug'] . '.html';
            header('Content-Type: text/html; charset=utf-8');
            header('Content-Disposition: attachment; filename="' . $fname . '"');
            echo $art['html'];
            exit;
        }
    }
    $liv_id = (int)($_GET['id'] ?? 0);
    $dl = isset($_GET['dl']) && $_GET['dl'] === '1';
    if ($liv_id) {
        $liv = $pdo->prepare("SELECT * FROM clients_web_livrables WHERE id=?");
        $liv->execute([$liv_id]);
        $liv = $liv->fetch();
        if ($liv) {
            $is_feed = $liv['type'] === 'feed';
            $is_zip  = $liv['type'] === 'zip';
            if ($is_zip) {
                $filename = 'site_' . preg_replace('/[^a-zA-Z0-9_-]/', '_', $liv['titre']) . '.zip';
                header('Content-Type: application/zip');
                header('Content-Disposition: attachment; filename="' . $filename . '"');
                echo base64_decode($liv['html']);
            } elseif ($is_feed) {
                $filename = preg_replace('/[^a-zA-Z0-9_-]/', '_', $liv['titre']) . '.xml';
                header('Content-Type: application/xml; charset=utf-8');
                if ($dl) header('Content-Disposition: attachment; filename="' . $filename . '"');
                echo $liv['html'];
            } else {
                $filename = preg_replace('/[^a-zA-Z0-9_-]/', '_', $liv['titre']) . '.html';
                header('Content-Type: text/html; charset=utf-8');
                if ($dl) header('Content-Disposition: attachment; filename="' . $filename . '"');
                echo $liv['html'];
            }
            exit;
        }
    }
    http_response_code(404);
    exit;
}

if ($page === 'clients_web') {
    $msg_cw   = $_GET['msg'] ?? '';
    $cw_id_v  = (int)($_GET['id'] ?? 0);
    $rapp_id_v = (int)($_GET['rapport_id'] ?? 0);

    // Charger tous les clients web
    $clients_cw = $pdo->query("SELECT c.*, (SELECT COUNT(*) FROM clients_web_rapports r WHERE r.client_id=c.id) as nb_rapports, (SELECT score_sante FROM clients_web_rapports r WHERE r.client_id=c.id ORDER BY r.created_at DESC LIMIT 1) as dernier_score FROM clients_web c WHERE c.archive=0 OR c.archive IS NULL ORDER BY c.created_at DESC")->fetchAll();

    adminHeader('Clients Web');
    echo '<div class="content">';

    $flash_cw = ['cree'=>['ok','Client cr.'],'modifie'=>['ok','Client mis  jour.'],'supprime'=>['ok','Client supprim.'],'archive'=>['ok','Client archiv.'],'desarchive'=>['ok','Client dsarchiv.'],'analyse_ok'=>['ok','Analyse termine  4 emails gnrs en brouillon.'],'valide'=>['ok','Email valid.'],'mensuel_ok'=>['ok','Rapport mensuel gnr.'],'relance_ok'=>['ok','Email de relance gnr en brouillon.'],'accompagnement_active'=>['ok','Accompagnement activ.'],'reconstruction_ok'=>['ok','Proposition de reconstruction gnre  email en brouillon.'],'livrables_ok'=>['ok','Briefing gnr  ZIP tlchargeable dans l\'historique.'],'produit_ok'=>['ok','Produit ajout.'],'code_source_ok'=>['ok','Code source sauvegard.'],'feed_ok'=>['ok','Feed Merchant Center gnr.'],'extraction_ok'=>['ok','Produits extraits et ajouts au catalogue.'],'extraction_vide'=>['err','Aucun produit trouv dans le code source.'],'logo_ok'=>['ok','Logo upload.'],'code_produit_ok'=>['ok','Code source produit sauvegard.'],'article_ok'=>['ok','Article de blog gnr.'],'err_csv'=>['err','CSV manquant ou client introuvable.'],
        // Phase 21
        'accompagnement_web_ok'=>['ok','Accompagnement accept  tableau 90 jours activ.'],'briefing_ok'=>['ok','Briefing gnr  ZIP tlchargeable.'],'tache_ok'=>['ok','Tche mise  jour.'],
        'facture_web_ok'=>['ok','Facture gnre  consultez et modifiez-la ci-dessous.'],'facture_web_envoyee'=>['ok','Facture envoye au client par email.'],'contrat_web_ok'=>['ok','Contrat gnr  consultez et modifiez-le ci-dessous.'],'contrat_web_envoye'=>['ok','Contrat envoy au client par email.']];
    if ($msg_cw && isset($flash_cw[$msg_cw])) echo '<div class="flash ' . $flash_cw[$msg_cw][0] . '">' . $flash_cw[$msg_cw][1] . '</div>';

    //  VUE FICHE CLIENT 
    if ($cw_id_v) {
        $cw_v = $pdo->prepare("SELECT * FROM clients_web WHERE id=?");
        $cw_v->execute([$cw_id_v]);
        $cw_v = $cw_v->fetch();
        if (!$cw_v) { header('Location: admin.php?page=clients_web'); exit; }

        // Emails brouillons et envoys
        // Charger emails  filtrs par rapport_id si disponible, sinon dernier rapport
        $dernier_rapport_id = $rapp_id_v;
        if (!$dernier_rapport_id) {
            $dr = $pdo->prepare("SELECT id FROM clients_web_rapports WHERE client_id=? ORDER BY created_at DESC LIMIT 1");
            $dr->execute([$cw_id_v]);
            $dr = $dr->fetch();
            $dernier_rapport_id = $dr ? $dr['id'] : 0;
        }
        $emails_cw = $pdo->prepare("SELECT * FROM clients_web_emails WHERE client_id=? AND (rapport_id=? OR rapport_id IS NULL OR type IN ('relance','mensuel','renouvellement','upsell')) ORDER BY created_at DESC");
        $emails_cw->execute([$cw_id_v, $dernier_rapport_id]);
        $emails_cw = $emails_cw->fetchAll();

        // Rapports
        $rapports_cw = $pdo->prepare("SELECT * FROM clients_web_rapports WHERE client_id=? ORDER BY created_at DESC");
        $rapports_cw->execute([$cw_id_v]);
        $rapports_cw = $rapports_cw->fetchAll();

        // Relances
        $relances_cw = $pdo->prepare("SELECT * FROM clients_web_relances WHERE client_id=?");
        $relances_cw->execute([$cw_id_v]);
        $relances_cw = $relances_cw->fetchAll();
        $relances_map = [];
        foreach ($relances_cw as $r) $relances_map[$r['etape']] = $r;

        $statuts_cw = ['actif'=>'Actif','en_attente'=>'En attente rponse','accompagnement'=>'Accompagnement actif','termine'=>'Termin'];
        ?>

        <div class="page-header">
          <div>

            <script>
            function handleCSVFiles(input) {
              if (!input.files || !input.files.length) return;
              var files = Array.from(input.files);
              document.getElementById('csv-filename').textContent = ' ' + files.length + ' fichier(s) slectionn(s)';
              document.getElementById('csv-upload-label').style.borderColor = 'var(--gold-border)';
              var filesList = document.getElementById('csv-files-list');
              filesList.textContent = files.map(function(f){ return f.name + ' (' + Math.round(f.size/1024) + ' Ko)'; }).join('  ');
              var contents = new Array(files.length);
              var loaded = 0;
              files.forEach(function(file, idx) {
                var reader = new FileReader();
                reader.onload = function(e) {
                  contents[idx] = '### FICHIER: ' + file.name + ' ###\n' + e.target.result;
                  loaded++;
                  if (loaded === files.length) {
                    document.getElementById('csv_data').value = contents.join('\n\n');
                  }
                };
                reader.onerror = function() {
                  contents[idx] = '### FICHIER: ' + file.name + '  erreur lecture ###';
                  loaded++;
                  if (loaded === files.length) {
                    document.getElementById('csv_data').value = contents.join('\n\n');
                  }
                };
                reader.readAsText(file, 'UTF-8');
              });
            }
            function handleCSVFile(input) { handleCSVFiles(input); }

            function setStep(id, status) {
              var el = document.getElementById(id);
              if (!el) return;
              var icon = el.querySelector('.step-icon');
              if (status === 'loading') { icon.textContent = ''; el.style.color = 'var(--gold)'; }
              else if (status === 'done') { icon.textContent = ''; el.style.color = 'var(--green)'; }
              else if (status === 'error') { icon.textContent = ''; el.style.color = 'var(--red)'; }
            }

            async function lancerAnalyseAjax() {
              var csv = document.getElementById('csv_data').value.trim();
              if (!csv) { alert('Veuillez slectionner un fichier CSV ou coller son contenu.'); return; }
              var clientId = <?= $cw_id_v ?>;
              var periode = document.getElementById('csv-periode') ? document.getElementById('csv-periode').value : '<?= date('Y') ?>';
              var action = '<?= $cw_v['accompagnement_actif'] ? 'generer_mensuel' : 'analyser_csv' ?>';

              document.getElementById('csv-form-zone').style.display = 'none';
              document.getElementById('analyse-progress').style.display = 'block';

              var steps = action === 'analyser_csv'
                ? ['step-analyse','step-e1','step-e2','step-e3','step-e4']
                : ['step-analyse','step-e1'];

              // Animer les tapes progressivement
              var delays = [0, 8000, 20000, 35000, 50000];
              steps.forEach(function(s, i) {
                setTimeout(function() { setStep(s, 'loading'); }, delays[i] || 0);
              });

              try {
                setStep('step-analyse', 'loading');
                var fd = new FormData();
                fd.append('action', action);
                fd.append('client_id', clientId);
                fd.append('periode', periode);
                fd.append('csv_data', csv);

                var resp = await fetch('analyse_csv.php', { method:'POST', body:fd });
                var data = await resp.json();

                if (data.success && data.redirect) {
                  steps.forEach(function(s) { setStep(s, 'done'); });
                  document.getElementById('step-done').style.display = 'block';
                  setTimeout(function() { window.location.href = data.redirect; }, 1500);
                } else {
                  setStep(steps[0], 'error');
                  document.getElementById('csv-form-zone').style.display = 'block';
                  document.getElementById('analyse-progress').style.display = 'none';
                  alert('Erreur : ' + (data.error || 'Vrifiez votre crdit API Anthropic sur console.anthropic.com'));
                }
              } catch(err) {
                steps.forEach(function(s) { setStep(s, 'error'); });
                document.getElementById('csv-form-zone').style.display = 'block';
                document.getElementById('analyse-progress').style.display = 'none';
                alert('Erreur rseau : ' + err.message);
              }
            }
            </script>

// PAGE FORMATION
// ============================================================
// ============================================================
// MODULE : SITES WEB 75K
// ============================================================
if ($page === 'sites_web_75k') {

    // --- Référence unique EP-{année}-Wxxx, partagée avec clients_web_factures
    //     pour que la numérotation reste cohérente dans toute la compta ---
    function genererReferenceSitesWeb75k(PDO $pdo): string {
        $annee = date('Y');
        $max = 0;
        foreach ([
            "SELECT reference FROM clients_web_factures WHERE reference LIKE 'EP-$annee-W%'",
            "SELECT reference FROM comptabilite_revenus_manuels WHERE reference LIKE 'EP-$annee-W%'",
        ] as $sql) {
            foreach ($pdo->query($sql)->fetchAll(PDO::FETCH_COLUMN) as $ref) {
                if (preg_match('/W(\d+)$/', $ref, $m)) {
                    $max = max($max, (int)$m[1]);
                }
            }
        }
        return "EP-$annee-W" . str_pad($max + 1, 3, '0', STR_PAD_LEFT);
    }

    // --- Création des tables si absentes (même pattern que connexion.php) ---
    $pdo->exec("CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS clients_site_web_75k (
        id INT AUTO_INCREMENT PRIMARY KEY,
        commande_id INT DEFAULT NULL,
        nom VARCHAR(190) NOT NULL,
        email VARCHAR(190) NOT NULL,
        whatsapp VARCHAR(30) NOT NULL,
        type_site VARCHAR(30) NOT NULL,
        domaine VARCHAR(190) DEFAULT NULL,
        date_livraison DATETIME DEFAULT NULL,
        date_expiration_domaine DATE DEFAULT NULL,
        url_site VARCHAR(255) DEFAULT NULL,
        infos_connexion TEXT DEFAULT NULL,
        statut ENUM('en_attente','acompte_envoye','site_livre','solde_recu','termine') NOT NULL DEFAULT 'en_attente',
        date_acompte DATETIME DEFAULT NULL,
        date_solde DATETIME DEFAULT NULL,
        email_acompte_envoye TINYINT(1) NOT NULL DEFAULT 0,
        email_livraison_envoye TINYINT(1) NOT NULL DEFAULT 0,
        email_solde_envoye TINYINT(1) NOT NULL DEFAULT 0,
        rappel_domaine_envoye TINYINT(1) NOT NULL DEFAULT 0,
        created_at DATETIME NOT NULL DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
        updated_at DATETIME NOT NULL DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP ON UPDATE CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
        UNIQUE KEY uniq_commande (commande_id)
    ) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8mb4");

    $pdo->exec("CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS clients_site_web_75k_emails (
        id INT AUTO_INCREMENT PRIMARY KEY,
        client_id INT NOT NULL,
        type VARCHAR(20) NOT NULL,
        sujet VARCHAR(255) NOT NULL,
        contenu_html LONGTEXT NOT NULL,
        reference VARCHAR(30) DEFAULT NULL,
        montant INT DEFAULT NULL,
        statut ENUM('brouillon','envoye') NOT NULL DEFAULT 'brouillon',
        envoye_at DATETIME DEFAULT NULL,
        created_at DATETIME NOT NULL DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP
    ) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8mb4");

    // ============================================================
    // ACTIONS POST
    // ============================================================
    if ($_SERVER['REQUEST_METHOD'] === 'POST') {

        // --- Importer les commandes non encore importées ---
        if (($_POST['do'] ?? '') === 'importer') {
            $deja = $pdo->query("SELECT commande_id FROM clients_site_web_75k WHERE commande_id IS NOT NULL")->fetchAll(PDO::FETCH_COLUMN);
            $sql = "SELECT * FROM commandes_site_web";
            if ($deja) {
                $in = implode(',', array_fill(0, count($deja), '?'));
                $sql .= " WHERE id NOT IN ($in)";
            }
            $stmt = $pdo->prepare($sql);
            $stmt->execute($deja);
            $nouveaux = $stmt->fetchAll();
            $ins = $pdo->prepare("INSERT INTO clients_site_web_75k (commande_id, nom, email, whatsapp, type_site, created_at) VALUES (?,?,?,?,?,NOW())");
            $nb = 0;
            foreach ($nouveaux as $c) {
                try {
                    $ins->execute([$c['id'], $c['nom'], $c['email'], $c['whatsapp'], $c['type_site']]);
                    $nb++;
                } catch (Exception $e) { /* doublon importé entre-temps (contrainte UNIQUE) — on ignore */ }
            }
            header('Location: admin.php?page=sites_web_75k&importes=' . $nb);
            exit;
        }

        // --- Ajouter un client manuellement (hors formulaire landing page) ---
        if (($_POST['do'] ?? '') === 'ajouter_manuel') {
            $pdo->prepare("INSERT INTO clients_site_web_75k (nom, email, whatsapp, type_site, created_at) VALUES (?,?,?,?,NOW())")
                ->execute([trim($_POST['nom']), trim($_POST['email']), trim($_POST['whatsapp']), trim($_POST['type_site'])]);
            header('Location: admin.php?page=sites_web_75k');
            exit;
        }

        // --- Mettre à jour la fiche (domaine, url, accès dépôt GitHub) ---
        if (($_POST['do'] ?? '') === 'maj_fiche') {
            $id = (int)$_POST['id'];
            $pdo->prepare("UPDATE clients_site_web_75k SET domaine=?, url_site=?, infos_connexion=?, updated_at=NOW() WHERE id=?")
                ->execute([trim($_POST['domaine']), trim($_POST['url_site']), trim($_POST['infos_connexion']), $id]);
            header('Location: admin.php?page=sites_web_75k&id=' . $id);
            exit;
        }

        // --- Générer email ACOMPTE (reçu fixe — pas d'IA sur un document factuel) ---
        if (($_POST['do'] ?? '') === 'generer_acompte') {
            $id = (int)$_POST['id'];
            $stmt = $pdo->prepare("SELECT * FROM clients_site_web_75k WHERE id=?");
            $stmt->execute([$id]);
            $c = $stmt->fetch();
            $ref = genererReferenceSitesWeb75k($pdo);
            $html = genererRecuPaiementHTML($c['nom'], $ref, 30000, 'Acompte — site web 75 000 FCFA (commande n°' . $c['id'] . ')');
            $pdo->prepare("INSERT INTO clients_site_web_75k_emails (client_id, type, sujet, contenu_html, reference, montant, statut, created_at) VALUES (?, 'acompte', ?, ?, ?, 30000, 'brouillon', NOW())")
                ->execute([$id, 'Confirmation de votre acompte — ' . $ref, $html, $ref]);
            header('Location: admin.php?page=sites_web_75k&id=' . $id);
            exit;
        }

        // --- Générer email SOLDE (reçu fixe) ---
        if (($_POST['do'] ?? '') === 'generer_solde') {
            $id = (int)$_POST['id'];
            $stmt = $pdo->prepare("SELECT * FROM clients_site_web_75k WHERE id=?");
            $stmt->execute([$id]);
            $c = $stmt->fetch();
            $ref = genererReferenceSitesWeb75k($pdo);
            $html = genererRecuPaiementHTML($c['nom'], $ref, 45000, 'Solde — site web 75 000 FCFA (commande n°' . $c['id'] . ')');
            $pdo->prepare("INSERT INTO clients_site_web_75k_emails (client_id, type, sujet, contenu_html, reference, montant, statut, created_at) VALUES (?, 'solde', ?, ?, ?, 45000, 'brouillon', NOW())")
                ->execute([$id, 'Confirmation de votre solde — ' . $ref, $html, $ref]);
            header('Location: admin.php?page=sites_web_75k&id=' . $id);
            exit;
        }

        // --- Générer email LIVRAISON (IA — seul email où la personnalisation apporte
        //     une vraie valeur ; toujours prévisualisé avant envoi, jamais automatique) ---
        if (($_POST['do'] ?? '') === 'generer_livraison') {
            $id = (int)$_POST['id'];
            $stmt = $pdo->prepare("SELECT * FROM clients_site_web_75k WHERE id=?");
            $stmt->execute([$id]);
            $c = $stmt->fetch();

            if (!$c['url_site']) {
                header('Location: admin.php?page=sites_web_75k&id=' . $id . '&erreur=url_manquante');
                exit;
            }

            $instructions = getEmailTemplateInstructions();
            $prompt = $instructions . "\n\nRedige un email de livraison de site web de K. Stephane a " . $c['nom'] . ".\n\n"
                . "Contexte : le site de type " . $c['type_site'] . " est termine et en ligne a l adresse https://" . $c['url_site'] . "\n\n"
                . "L email doit :\n"
                . "- Annoncer que le site est en ligne, avec enthousiasme sobre\n"
                . "- Donner le lien du site en evidence : https://" . $c['url_site'] . "\n"
                . "- Expliquer en 2-3 points simples comment demander une modification de contenu (tarif : 3000 FCFA texte, 2000 FCFA ajout produit)\n"
                . "- Rappeler que 7 jours de corrections techniques gratuites suivent la livraison (bugs uniquement, pas les modifications de contenu)\n"
                . "- Demander le solde de 45 000 FCFA pour finaliser\n"
                . "- Signer K. Stephane — ePerformance";

            $html = callAI($prompt, 2000, DEEPSEEK_MODEL);
            $ref = genererReferenceSitesWeb75k($pdo);

            $pdo->prepare("INSERT INTO clients_site_web_75k_emails (client_id, type, sujet, contenu_html, reference, statut, created_at) VALUES (?, 'livraison', ?, ?, ?, 'brouillon', NOW())")
                ->execute([$id, 'Votre site est en ligne !', $html, $ref]);
            header('Location: admin.php?page=sites_web_75k&id=' . $id);
            exit;
        }

        // --- Sauvegarder une édition d'email (avant envoi) ---
        if (($_POST['do'] ?? '') === 'sauvegarder_email') {
            $pdo->prepare("UPDATE clients_site_web_75k_emails SET sujet=?, contenu_html=? WHERE id=?")
                ->execute([trim($_POST['sujet']), $_POST['contenu_html'], (int)$_POST['email_id']]);
            header('Location: admin.php?page=sites_web_75k&id=' . (int)$_POST['id']);
            exit;
        }

        // --- Envoyer l'email : met à jour le statut client + alimente la comptabilité
        //     existante pour acompte/solde (comptabilite_revenus_manuels) ---
        if (($_POST['do'] ?? '') === 'envoyer_email') {
            $email_id = (int)$_POST['email_id'];
            $client_id = (int)$_POST['id'];

            $stmt = $pdo->prepare("SELECT e.*, c.nom, c.email FROM clients_site_web_75k_emails e JOIN clients_site_web_75k c ON c.id=e.client_id WHERE e.id=?");
            $stmt->execute([$email_id]);
            $email = $stmt->fetch();

            if ($email && $email['statut'] === 'envoye') {
                // Déjà envoyé — on ignore silencieusement plutôt que de renvoyer l'email
                // et de dupliquer l'écriture comptable si la requête est rejouée.
                header('Location: admin.php?page=sites_web_75k&id=' . $client_id);
                exit;
            }

            if ($email) {
                sendBrevo($email['email'], $email['nom'], $email['sujet'], $email['contenu_html']);
                $pdo->prepare("UPDATE clients_site_web_75k_emails SET statut='envoye', envoye_at=NOW() WHERE id=?")->execute([$email_id]);

                if ($email['type'] === 'acompte') {
                    $pdo->prepare("UPDATE clients_site_web_75k SET statut='acompte_envoye', date_acompte=NOW(), email_acompte_envoye=1, updated_at=NOW() WHERE id=?")->execute([$client_id]);
                    $pdo->prepare("INSERT INTO comptabilite_revenus_manuels (mois, libelle, categorie, montant, client_nom, reference, date_paiement, created_at) VALUES (?,?,?,?,?,?,CURDATE(),NOW())")
                        ->execute([date('Y-m'), 'Acompte site web 75k — ' . $email['nom'], 'Site web 75k', $email['montant'], $email['nom'], $email['reference']]);
                    sendTelegram("💰 <b>Acompte reçu — Site web 75k</b>\n👤 " . $email['nom'] . "\n💵 30 000 FCFA\n🧾 " . $email['reference']);
                }
                if ($email['type'] === 'livraison') {
                    // Date de départ des 7 jours de support ET de l'expiration domaine à 1 an,
                    // calculée automatiquement pour ne pas dépendre d'une saisie manuelle oubliable.
                    $pdo->prepare("UPDATE clients_site_web_75k SET statut='site_livre', date_livraison=NOW(), date_expiration_domaine=DATE_ADD(NOW(), INTERVAL 1 YEAR), email_livraison_envoye=1, updated_at=NOW() WHERE id=?")->execute([$client_id]);
                    sendTelegram("🚀 <b>Site livré</b>\n👤 " . $email['nom'] . "\n🌍 https://" . htmlspecialchars($_POST['url_rappel'] ?? '') );
                }
                if ($email['type'] === 'solde') {
                    $pdo->prepare("UPDATE clients_site_web_75k SET statut='solde_recu', date_solde=NOW(), email_solde_envoye=1, updated_at=NOW() WHERE id=?")->execute([$client_id]);
                    $pdo->prepare("INSERT INTO comptabilite_revenus_manuels (mois, libelle, categorie, montant, client_nom, reference, date_paiement, created_at) VALUES (?,?,?,?,?,?,CURDATE(),NOW())")
                        ->execute([date('Y-m'), 'Solde site web 75k — ' . $email['nom'], 'Site web 75k', $email['montant'], $email['nom'], $email['reference']]);
                    sendTelegram("✅ <b>Solde reçu — Site web 75k</b>\n👤 " . $email['nom'] . "\n💵 45 000 FCFA\n🧾 " . $email['reference'] . "\n🏁 Commande terminée");
                    $pdo->prepare("UPDATE clients_site_web_75k SET statut='termine' WHERE id=?")->execute([$client_id]);
                }
            }
            header('Location: admin.php?page=sites_web_75k&id=' . $client_id);
            exit;
        }

        // --- Supprimer un client ---
        if (($_POST['do'] ?? '') === 'supprimer') {
            $id = (int)$_POST['id'];
            $pdo->prepare("DELETE FROM clients_site_web_75k_emails WHERE client_id=?")->execute([$id]);
            $pdo->prepare("DELETE FROM clients_site_web_75k WHERE id=?")->execute([$id]);
            header('Location: admin.php?page=sites_web_75k');
            exit;
        }
    }

          <?php endif; ?>

          <!-- Infos client -->
          <div style="background:var(--card);border:1px solid var(--border);border-radius:16px;padding:1.4rem;margin-bottom:1.2rem">

            <form method="POST">
              <input type="hidden" name="do" value="maj_fiche">
              <input type="hidden" name="id" value="<?= $id ?>">
              <label style="display:block;font-size:.8rem;color:var(--soft);margin-bottom:.3rem">Nom de domaine</label>
              <input type="text" name="domaine" value="<?= htmlspecialchars($c['domaine'] ?? '') ?>" style="width:100%;padding:.6rem;margin-bottom:.8rem;background:var(--bg);border:1px solid var(--border2);border-radius:8px;color:var(--text)">
              <label style="display:block;font-size:.8rem;color:var(--soft);margin-bottom:.3rem">URL du site livré (sans https://)</label>
              <input type="text" name="url_site" value="<?= htmlspecialchars($c['url_site'] ?? '') ?>" placeholder="monsite.ci" style="width:100%;padding:.6rem;margin-bottom:.8rem;background:var(--bg);border:1px solid var(--border2);border-radius:8px;color:var(--text)">

          <!-- 3 sections email -->

if ($page === 'formation') {

    // Stats globales formation
    $stats_fm = $pdo->query("SELECT

// PAGE LISTE  TABLEAU DE BORD PRINCIPAL
// ============================================================
$filtre = $_GET['filtre'] ?? 'tous';
$filtres_valides = ['en_attente', 'accepte', 'refuse', 'alumni'];
$where = in_array($filtre, $filtres_valides) ? "WHERE c.statut = " . $pdo->quote($filtre) : '';
$candidats = $pdo->query("
    SELECT c.*, d.score, d.cac, d.ltv, d.ratio_ltv_cac, d.recommandation,
           JSON_UNQUOTE(JSON_EXTRACT(d.donnees, '$.budget_accompagnement')) as budget_acc,
           c.score_risque, c.niveau_risque
    FROM candidats c
    LEFT JOIN diagnostics d ON d.candidat_id = c.id
    $where
    ORDER BY c.created_at DESC
")->fetchAll();
$stats = $pdo->query("SELECT COUNT(*) as total, SUM(statut='en_attente') as attente, SUM(statut='accepte') as accepte, SUM(statut='refuse') as refuse, SUM(statut='alumni') as alumni FROM candidats")->fetch();
$budgetLabels = ['moins_100k' => '< 100k', '100_300k' => '100300k', '300_600k' => '300600k', 'plus_600k' => '> 600k', 'ne_sait_pas' => 'NSP'];
?>
<!DOCTYPE html>
<html lang="fr">
<head>
<meta charset="utf-8"/>

  </div>
  <?php

echo '<div class="table-wrap"><table>';
echo '<thead><tr><th>Origine</th><th>Client</th><th>Score</th><th>Pipeline</th><th>Date début</th><th>Actions</th></tr></thead><tbody>';

if (empty($vue_unifiee)) {

} else {
    foreach ($vue_unifiee as $vu) {
        $lien = $vu['origine'] === 'candidat' ? "admin.php?page=client&id={$vu['id']}" : "admin.php?page=clients_web&id={$vu['id']}";

?>

  <!--  PIPELINE PROSPECTS  -->
  <div class="section-title" style="margin-top:1.5rem">Pipeline prospects
    <span style="font-size:.75rem;color:var(--muted);font-weight:400;margin-left:.5rem">Vue par statut</span>
  </div>
  <?php
  $pipe_cols = [
    'en_attente'  => ['label'=>'En attente',     'color'=>'#f0a832', 'bg'=>'rgba(240,168,50,.08)',  'border'=>'rgba(240,168,50,.25)'],
    'contacte'    => ['label'=>'Contact',        'color'=>'#6b9ef8', 'bg'=>'rgba(107,158,248,.08)', 'border'=>'rgba(107,158,248,.25)'],
    'appel_prevu' => ['label'=>'Appel planifi',  'color'=>'#c9a96e', 'bg'=>'rgba(201,169,110,.08)', 'border'=>'rgba(201,169,110,.25)'],
    'accepte'     => ['label'=>'Accept',         'color'=>'#6fcf8a', 'bg'=>'rgba(111,207,138,.08)', 'border'=>'rgba(111,207,138,.25)'],
  ];
  // Rcuprer tous les prospects actifs (hors refuss et alumni)
  $pipe_prospects = $pdo->query("SELECT id, nom, entreprise, secteur, score, whatsapp, statut, pipeline_statut, created_at FROM candidats WHERE statut NOT IN('refuse','alumni') ORDER BY created_at DESC")->fetchAll();
  // Grouper par pipeline_statut (fallback sur statut si pipeline_statut est null)
  $grouped = ['en_attente'=>[], 'contacte'=>[], 'appel_prevu'=>[], 'accepte'=>[]];
  foreach ($pipe_prospects as $pp) {
    $ps = $pp['pipeline_statut'] ?? ($pp['statut'] === 'accepte' ? 'accepte' : 'en_attente');
    if (!isset($grouped[$ps])) $ps = 'en_attente';
    $grouped[$ps][] = $pp;
  }
  $secteur_icons = ['mlm'=>'','ecommerce'=>'','formation'=>'','cosmetiques'=>'','restauration'=>'','immobilier'=>'','services'=>'','autre'=>''];
  ?>
  <div style="display:grid;grid-template-columns:repeat(4,1fr);gap:.8rem;margin-bottom:1.5rem">
  <?php foreach ($pipe_cols as $pipe_key => $pipe_cfg): ?>
    <div style="background:<?= $pipe_cfg['bg'] ?>;border:1px solid <?= $pipe_cfg['border'] ?>;border-radius:14px;padding:1rem">
      <div style="display:flex;align-items:center;justify-content:space-between;margin-bottom:.8rem">
        <span style="font-size:.72rem;text-transform:uppercase;letter-spacing:.1em;color:<?= $pipe_cfg['color'] ?>;font-weight:700"><?= $pipe_cfg['label'] ?></span>
        <span style="font-family:'Cormorant Garamond',serif;font-size:1.3rem;font-weight:700;color:<?= $pipe_cfg['color'] ?>"><?= count($grouped[$pipe_key]) ?></span>
      </div>
      <div style="display:flex;flex-direction:column;gap:.5rem">
      <?php if (empty($grouped[$pipe_key])): ?>
        <div style="font-size:.78rem;color:var(--muted);font-style:italic;padding:.4rem 0">Aucun prospect</div>
      <?php else: ?>
      <?php foreach ($grouped[$pipe_key] as $pp):
        $tel = preg_replace('/\D/', '', $pp['whatsapp'] ?? '');
        $icon = $secteur_icons[$pp['secteur']??'autre'] ?? '';
      ?>
        <div style="background:var(--card);border:1px solid var(--border);border-radius:10px;padding:.65rem .8rem">
          <div style="display:flex;align-items:center;justify-content:space-between;gap:.4rem;margin-bottom:.3rem">
            <span style="font-size:.82rem;font-weight:600;color:var(--text);white-space:nowrap;overflow:hidden;text-overflow:ellipsis"><?= htmlspecialchars($pp['nom']) ?></span>
            <span style="font-size:.7rem"><?= $icon ?></span>
          </div>
          <div style="font-size:.72rem;color:var(--muted);margin-bottom:.45rem"><?= htmlspecialchars($pp['entreprise'] ?? $pp['secteur'] ?? '') ?></div>
          <div style="display:flex;align-items:center;justify-content:space-between;gap:.4rem">
            <span style="font-size:.72rem;font-weight:700;color:<?= ($pp['score']??0)>=75?'#6fcf8a':(($pp['score']??0)>=50?'#c9a96e':'#e07070') ?>"><?= $pp['score'] ?? '' ?>/100</span>
            <div style="display:flex;gap:.3rem">
              <a href="?page=client&id=<?= $pp['id'] ?>" style="font-size:.68rem;padding:.2rem .5rem;border-radius:6px;background:var(--gold-bg);color:var(--gold);border:1px solid var(--gold-border);text-decoration:none">Fiche</a>
              <?php if ($tel): ?><a href="https://wa.me/<?= $tel ?>" target="_blank" style="font-size:.68rem;padding:.2rem .5rem;border-radius:6px;background:rgba(37,211,102,.1);color:#25D366;border:1px solid rgba(37,211,102,.3);text-decoration:none">WA</a><?php endif; ?>
            </div>
          </div>
          <!-- Dplacer vers colonne -->
          <form method="POST" style="margin-top:.4rem">
            <input type="hidden" name="action" value="changer_pipeline"/>
            <input type="hidden" name="candidat_id" value="<?= $pp['id'] ?>"/>
            <select name="pipeline_statut" onchange="this.form.submit()" style="width:100%;background:#0a0a0e;border:1px solid var(--border);border-radius:6px;color:var(--muted);font-size:.68rem;padding:.2rem .4rem;cursor:pointer;outline:none">
              <option value=""> Dplacer vers</option>
              <?php foreach ($pipe_cols as $pk => $pc): if ($pk === $pipe_key) continue; ?>
              <option value="<?= $pk ?>"><?= $pc['label'] ?></option>
              <?php endforeach; ?>
            </select>
          </form>
        </div>
      <?php endforeach; ?>
      <?php endif; ?>
      </div>
    </div>
  <?php endforeach; ?>
  </div>

  <div class="section-title">Candidatures
    <span style="font-size:.75rem;color:var(--muted);font-weight:400;margin-left:.5rem">Vue liste complte</span>

  <?php if (empty($candidats)): ?>
  <div class="empty-state">Aucune candidature.</div>

      $tel = preg_replace('/\D/', '', $c['whatsapp'] ?? '');
      $wa_msg = $c['statut'] === 'accepte'
        ? "Bonjour " . $c['nom'] . " \n\nVotre candidature ePerformance a t accepte.\nConnectez-vous : https://api.eperformance.pro/connexion.php\n\nK. Stphane  ePerformance"

    ?>

      <td>
        <div style="font-weight:600"><?= htmlspecialchars($c['nom']) ?></div>
        <div style="font-size:.78rem;color:var(--muted)"><?= htmlspecialchars($c['email']) ?></div>
      </td>
      <td style="color:var(--soft)"><?= htmlspecialchars($c['secteur'] ?? '') ?></td>
      <td><span class="score-chip" style="color:<?= ($c['score']??0)>=75?'#6fcf8a':(($c['score']??0)>=50?'#c9a96e':'#e07070') ?>"><?= $c['score'] ?? '' ?><?= $c['score'] ? '/100' : '' ?></span></td>
      <td><?php if ($c['budget_acc']): ?><span class="budget-chip"><?= $budgetLabels[$c['budget_acc']] ?? $c['budget_acc'] ?></span><?php else: ?><?php endif; ?></td>
      <td><span class="badge <?= $c['statut'] ?>"><?= ['en_attente'=>'En attente','accepte'=>'Accept','refuse'=>'Refus','alumni'=>'Alumni'][$c['statut']]??$c['statut'] ?></span></td>
      <td style="color:var(--muted);font-size:.8rem"><?= date('d/m/Y', strtotime($c['created_at'])) ?></td>

        <div class="actions">
          <a href="?page=client&id=<?= $c['id'] ?>" class="btn-sm btn-detail">Grer</a>
          <?php if ($tel): ?><a href="https://wa.me/<?= $tel ?>?text=<?= rawurlencode($wa_msg) ?>" target="_blank" class="btn-sm btn-wa">WA</a><?php endif; ?>
          <?php if ($c['statut'] !== 'accepte'): ?>
          <form method="POST" style="margin:0;display:inline"><input type="hidden" name="candidat_id" value="<?= $c['id'] ?>"/><input type="hidden" name="action" value="accepter"/><button type="submit" class="btn-sm btn-accepter">Accepter</button></form>
          <?php endif; ?>
          <?php if ($c['statut'] !== 'refuse'): ?>
          <form method="POST" style="margin:0;display:inline"><input type="hidden" name="candidat_id" value="<?= $c['id'] ?>"/><input type="hidden" name="action" value="refuser"/><button type="submit" class="btn-sm btn-refuser">Refuser</button></form>
          <?php endif; ?>
